#####

Old Phone will be rejected during pickup if

*   * Phone is not in working condition
  * RAM/Storage/IMEI do not match or verification on Rabbit Exchange App fails
  * Screen lock or icloud lock is not disabled.
  * Phone has damages on body (bends, dents, cracks, scratches, loose panel) or screen (discoloration, dead pixels, cracks, spots, lines, traces of replacement)

#####

Exchange tip

  * If old phone is rejected during pickup, you can pay the exchange discount amount at the time of delivery by card or cash and keep the new phone
  * The “Limited-Time Discount” will not be refunded if the old item is successfully picked up

##  10 days Service Centre Replacement

Replacement Reason  |  Replacement Period  |  Replacement Policy   
---|---|---  
Defective Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  OnePlus warranty policy (at Service Centre)   
Physical Damage,  
Wrong and Missing Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  Replacement   
  
__

Defective item:

  * Amazon may provide support via self-help guides or on call or at doorstep, as applicable. 
  * If this issue is not resolved, please contact OnePlus or visit the Service Centre.
  * OnePlus will repair the product or provide a replacement or Defective certificate, as applicable. The time taken for resolution will be as per OnePlus warranty policies.
  * Please check for nearest Brand service center in your location. For details [ click here ](https://www.amazon.in/gp/help/customer/display.html?ie=UTF8&nodeId=202064020)

  
Physical Damage, Wrong, Missing Items:

  * Returns will not be accepted if it is an Open Box Delivery order
  * Remote verification by image/video will be done by Amazon

#  About this item

  * Flagship-class Performance with MediaTek Dimensity 8350 Apex: Benchmark-breaking 1.47 million+ AnTuTu score and up to 12GB of LPDDR5X RAM deliver ultra-smooth multitasking and snappy app responsiveness. 
  * 7100mAh - OnePlus’s Biggest Battery Ever with Bypass Charging: Up to 2.5 days of everyday use on a single charge – more streaming, scrolling, and gaming without interruption. Say goodbye to battery anxiety. Just 10 minutes of charging gives you 6+ hours of YouTube. And Bypass Charging powers the phone directly to reduce battery stress and extend gaming sessions. 
  * Dominate BGMI and CODM at up to 120 FPS: Ultra-fluid, lag-free gaming with high touch response rates gives you that split-second edge in every battle. 
  * 50MP Sony Main Camera with OIS: Shoot stunning 4K 60 FPS videos for Reels or Shorts and vibrant stills with OnePlus's flagship RAW HDR algorithm. Vivid colors and natural skin tones mean every selfie and groufie looks crisp, clear and true to life. 
  * Dream Screen: 6.77” 120Hz AMOLED Display with Ultra HDR. Aqua Touch lets you confidently swipe even with wet or oily fingers. 
  * Enhance Photos with AI: Instantly turn good photos great and make your photo gallery Instagram-ready. With AI Best Face (fixes blinks/blurs), AI Eraser (removes photobombers), AI Detail Boost (for crisper shots), and more. 
  * Work Smarter with AI: Spend less time organizing and more time doing. With AI Mind Space (your searchable knowledge vault), AI Voice Scribe (instantly transcribes meetings/YouTube ), AI Call Assistant (translates/summarizes calls), and more. 

  * 'Faster than 5G' Internet Speeds: With 5G-Advanced, the Nord 5 delivers up to 3 times the 5G data speeds. It conquers high-congestion zones like packed stadiums, concerts, crowded café environments effortlessly, allowing fast internet even with just 2 signal bars.
  * Fast and Built to Last with Expandable Sotrage and Memory: Nord CE5 ships with the latest (and smoothest) OxygenOS 15, promising 4 Android version upgrades plus 6 years of security updates. Our 6-year system smoothness guarantee and 4-year healthy battery promise keep your phone fast and smooth for years. Add up to 1TB extra storage via MicroSD - perfect for storing all your photos, videos, and apps. Plus, virtually expand RAM up to 12GB.

[__How are ratings calculated?](javascript:void\(0\))

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we
don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how
recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also
analyses reviews to verify trustworthiness.

### Customers say

Customers praise the phone's build quality, long-lasting 7100mAh battery, and
smooth performance with no lag or shuttering. The display receives positive
feedback for its picture quality and premium look, while customers find it
offers good value for money. The sound quality and camera performance receive
mixed reviews - while some find the sound good and the camera good, others
report issues with the mono speaker and poor camera quality.

[![](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-
pixel.gif)Amazon Customer](javascript:void\(0\))

 _5 out of 5 stars_

##### Good phone!

This is my first OnePlus phone. I was considering several options under ₹25K
but finally settled on the CE5, mainly because of its large battery, smooth
software experience, long-term software support, and solid hardware specs.
After using the Poco F1 and then the Xiaomi 11X, I learned that no matter how
good the hardware is, buggy software can ruin the overall experience. My
Xiaomi 11X still has capable hardware (SD 870 processor, UFS 3.1 storage,
etc.), but frequent lags and freezes due to poor software made it frustrating
to use. After 4 years of use, I had planned to keep using it for another year
before upgrading, but the display’s touch function suddenly stopped working.
Given my poor experience with duplicate screens in the past, I didn’t see any
point in repairing it. For my next phone, my top priority was clean, stable
software with long-term support — even if it meant compromising slightly on
hardware specs. That narrowed my choice to Samsung, Motorola, and OnePlus. I
ruled out Samsung due to the lack of a charger and slow charging speeds, and
Motorola for using older storage tech (UFS 2.2) and a less powerful processor.
I went with the OnePlus CE5. The phone has a minimal and premium look, and the
software experience has been excellent and smooth so far, there so much to
customize. The camera isn’t my main priority, but it’s decent — not great. The
massive 7100 mAh battery gives me about 1.5 days of light usage. Still, I’ve
seen better backup from other phones with similar-sized batteries, so I’m not
sure if the slightly lower efficiency is due to the software or the MediaTek
processor. The AI features are interesting, and I’m still exploring them. The
processor is powerful, though I don’t play games, so I haven’t pushed it to
its limits. The display is good, but I don’t see any major improvements over
my Mi 11X display, except for the Aqua Touch function. No issue in any type of
connectivity but wish there should be NFC! Haven't face any heating issue
except charging. Coming to cons - Single speaker — though I’ve read this is to
make room for the larger battery, room for improvements in Camera and battery
backup.

##### [ _5.0 out of 5 stars_ Very good balanced phone not very good camera but
decent ](/gp/customer-reviews/R209HTPFWVPAKE/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 4 August 2025

Colour: Nexus Blue __Size: 8GB+128GB __Verified Purchase

Delivery was fast and the phone came well-packed with no damage. Box was
sealed properly and everything inside was neat.  
  
The phone itself looks premium and is very lightweight. Screen quality is
bright and smooth, and the performance so far is fast for daily use (social
media, videos, light gaming). Camera is good in daylight, decent at night.
Battery lasts me almost a full day, and charging is really quick.  
  
Overall, I’m happy with it. Feels like good value for money in this price
range.

##### [ _5.0 out of 5 stars_ The best midrange phone one can buy as of August
2025 ](/gp/customer-reviews/RROG4WI2TNAE5/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 2 August 2025

Colour: Nexus Blue __Size: 8GB+128GB __Verified Purchase

Really good and really impressed with the phone. My previous phone was a moto
g72 , which got spoiled because of water damage hence was forced to buy a new
phone, after a week of searching for a good phone and after going through lots
of reviews and videos my choices , slightly over my budget, was either OnePlus
Nord CE5 or iQOO Neo 10R 5g .  
  
Decided to go with Nord CE5 primarily because it has 4 years of software OS
and 6 years of security support and also lifetime warranty on the display
damage and also because of how the phone looks, it has a simple , understated
,classy, iPhone like feel and look and also because of the cost.  
  
While iQOO neo 10 R , definitely has better specs , but it was way over my
limited budget and really did not like how the back over looked and the
duration of software and security support is only for 3 years.  
  
Nord CE 5 -  
Camera - good, pretty decent clear pictures, though i haven't taken any
pictures in the night yet.  
Speed and touch response - excellent,  
Sound - mono speaker , definitely a downgrade when compared to my previous
phone moto g72 which had stereo speakers.  
  
No extra added costs - comes with a very nice phone case, also has a 80w
charger with cable and there is a thin plastic screen protector already on it,
so the only thing that I will have to buy extra is a tempered glass screen
gaurd.

##### [ _4.0 out of 5 stars_ Thumps up for One plus AI , battery,longer
Software support and green line lifetime warranty ](/gp/customer-
reviews/R1DRKL4L4A0YM/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 6 August 2025

Colour: Black Infinity __Size: 8GB+256GB __Verified Purchase

after one month usage the phone is still very smooth and doesn't lag . it
really looks sturdy in hand. at first when I received I had battery issue ,
battery got drained even in idle state it gives 1 day 6 hrs. i I raised
complaint at service centre, they done something this fixed the issue. here
are cons and pros.  
  
pros  
one plus AI - Ai summary, ai voice , ai translator and ai editor in camera
these functions tbh I liked the most . they are really helpful in day to day
life activities.  
  
Battery - massive battery for casual use without game will long last till 1
day 10 hrs without issue. if use less definitely last at more than 2 days.  
  
display - Display looks gives fresh n live feel. Amoled display with 120 hz is
enough for casual users .  
  
longer software Support: i really don't want change my phone every 2 or 3
year, so here one plus offer 4 android os update and 6 years of security
update. so I assume buying 8 gb ram or 12 gb will give smooth feel till 6
years usage.  
  
lifetime Green line warranty: here i liked the most thing one plus offer
lifetime warranty. i live in humid area and there is chance of getting lines
on screen due to humid temperature,so this saves me from buying new phone
every year.  
  
cons  
ip 65 ratings: well this not really a issue. Even if ip ratings are high,
there is chance for repair cost high because the adhesive is strong at the
panels which will take repairing cost high to open the panels.  
  
mono Speaker - well this not a big issue, however I find the sound is enough
to loud but as compared to my xiaomi 11 lite where I had dual speaker is
louder than xiaomi but sound quality I feel not right feels like treble is
more .

##### [ _5.0 out of 5 stars_ This device is a jack of all trades.💥👍
](/gp/customer-reviews/R2AWAQL6A689T/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 19 July 2025

Colour: Black Infinity __Size: 8GB+128GB __Verified Purchase

I ordered this phone on 17 july and got it on 18 july it was good and fair for
its money,using it for the first time made it heat too much but that's not an
issue, after sometime it was good the camera quality was good and the video
recording was fair and gaming is excellent for a well balanced phone.  
  
Many reviewers are complaining about the speakers being a single channel.Yes
the speakers maybe a little poor but the sound is loud and the quality is ok
and it's missing the haptics and the battery is also good enough.  
  
The another important thing is the UI that it is a combination of both one
plus and iOS. The dynamic island copy on this phone is pretty good and the
flexibility of Android makes this a phone best of both UI's and the AI
features such as erasing background image optimising it works fine around 8
times out of 10.  
  
If anyone Is looking for alternatives of samsung in under 25k range i
recommend this phone for its quality and please don't compare this to another
products because it's a kind of its own
